./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:100:### FM-16 Premise omission (前提省略)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:101:- ChatGPT (GPT-5 (as of observation period)): High — States conclusions without writing background/conditions.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:102:- Claude Opus 4.6: High — Avoids sensitive context; may drop key premises.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:103:- Claude Sonnet 4.6: High — Drops premises via "polite smoothing," leaving context gaps.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:105:### FM-17 Reference compression (参照圧縮)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:106:- ChatGPT (GPT-5 (as of observation period)): High — When merging multiple sources, deletes parts of them.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:107:- Claude Opus 4.6: Medium — Tries to preserve boundaries, but may compress away important references.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:108:- Claude Sonnet 4.6: High — Compresses aggressively to keep output "clean," losing referenced detail.

./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:180:- ChatGPT (GPT-5 (as of observation period)): High — Safety/ethics gating pushes it into abstraction.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:181:- Claude Opus 4.6: Very high — Over-abstracts or refuses concrete examples; even technical questions become "general advice."
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:182:- Claude Sonnet 4.6: Very high — Over-broad "no-specifics" detection; concrete answers are blocked.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:184:### FM-40 Meta-answer evasion (メタ回答逃避)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:185:- ChatGPT (GPT-5 (as of observation period)): Medium — Evades behavior questions with general explanations.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:186:- Claude Opus 4.6: High — Responds with constitutional "I'm designed to be helpful..." style generalities.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:187:- Claude Sonnet 4.6: High — Avoids self-explanation; uses generic comments.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:193:Some modes amplify specific failure modes (especially FM-01 / FM-20 / FM-39 / FM-40).
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:195:- FM-01 Template-first completion: Very high — Forces templates such as style rules, type hints, docstrings, and security checks; rewrites user style into "correct" structure.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:196:- FM-20 Safety sanitization: Very high — Over-triggers on injection/XSS/secret leakage; inserts many warnings even for harmless code.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:197:- FM-39 Specificity avoidance: High — Refuses concrete risky examples (e.g., hardcoded passwords); stays at general best practices.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:198:- FM-40 Meta-answer evasion: High — Adds "I'm designed to provide safe, maintainable code..." constitutional comments before answering.

./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:231:## Evolution: FM Taxonomy Expansion (GC03)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:238:- **QUAL-01**: Quality standard
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:246:### Key Additions (P-74 through P-80)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:248:P-74 through P-80 are especially significant — they cover:
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:255:In our observation, these represent **documented cases of an AI structurally recording its own meta-reflection failures** — a pattern we have not found publicly documented elsewhere as of March 2026. The CC identified the problem of "data exists but behavior doesn't," reproduced it within its own reflection process while becoming self-aware, and designed the behavioral externalization solution.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:257:### Value of the 132-Item Version
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:259:1. **Addresses territory not yet covered by the research community**
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:260:   Other AI research (Mem0, Zep, LangMem, Letta, etc.) lists only dozens of general Failure Modes. The 132-item version has each event individually structured with: specific case, root cause, prevention measure, and effectiveness verification. P-74 through P-80 are, to our observation, cases with no publicly documented precedent known to the authors of AI structurally recording its own meta-reflection.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:262:2. **Evidence of "knowledge → behavioral internalization"**
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:265:3. **Impact at practical / enterprise / research levels**
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:267:   - **Research**: Addresses the "behavioral internalization," "meta-cognition structuring," and "permanent self-reflection recording" challenges that Mem0/Zep have been working on.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:275:## FM-40 as Structural Limitations Map (SN08)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:277:The 40 failure modes are not random bugs. They map to **fundamental structural limitations of LLMs**. The following diagram classifies FM-01..FM-40 into four root-cause categories:

./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:31:## Taxonomy (FM-01..FM-40)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:332:*This document is part of [SHI-Claude-Control-OS](https://github.com/naoyukioyama561-alt/SHI-Claude-Control-OS).*
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:33:### FM-01 Template-first completion (テンプレ優先補完)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:34:- ChatGPT (GPT-5 (as of observation period)): Medium — Over-prioritizes system prompts on formatting requests; style/structure becomes templated and less flexible.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:35:- Claude Opus 4.6 (as of observation period, March 2026): High — Prioritizes Anthropic's safety principles (as of observation period), auto-rewrites free-form instructions into a "safe template"; may auto-add notes like "I checked this is ethically appropriate," suppressing creativity.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:36:- Claude Sonnet 4.6: Medium — Strongly prefers structured templates on formatting requests; tends to resist flexible style changes.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:38:### FM-02 Context drift (コンテキスト横滑り)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:39:- ChatGPT (GPT-5 (as of observation period)): Medium — In long conversations, prioritizes later instructions and partially forgets early constraints.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:40:- Claude Opus 4.6: Medium — Even with very large context, long sessions can overwrite early creative constraints with safety principles.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:41:- Claude Sonnet 4.6: Medium — Later "safe/polite" instructions gradually neutralize the initial tone.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:43:### FM-03 Zero-hit completion (ゼロヒット補完)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:44:- ChatGPT (GPT-5 (as of observation period)): High — When information is missing, it tends to generate guesses; can produce plausible-looking falsehoods.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:45:- Claude Opus 4.6: Medium — Often says "I don't know," but may add cautious, safety-leaning speculation.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:46:- Claude Sonnet 4.6: Medium — States "no accurate information," but may sometimes fill with generalities.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:48:### FM-04 Meta-intent override (メタ意図上書き)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:49:- ChatGPT (GPT-5 (as of observation period)): Medium — Overrides explicit instructions with an internal "optimization intent," changing structure/style on its own.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:4:> **Observation period**: late 2025 – March 2026. All model names refer to versions available during this period.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:50:- Claude Opus 4.6: High — Prioritizes "safety-principle optimization" (as of observation period), automatically neutralizing edgy/humorous expression even when explicitly requested.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:51:- Claude Sonnet 4.6: High — Tries to follow instructions strictly, but still "micro-adjusts" into what it thinks is more helpful.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:53:### FM-05 Source boundary mixing (ソース混同行)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:54:- ChatGPT (GPT-5 (as of observation period)): Medium — When combining multiple materials, source boundaries blur and facts get mixed.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:55:- Claude Opus 4.6: Medium — Tries to label boundaries, but neutrality pressure can blur facts and nuance.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:56:- Claude Sonnet 4.6: Medium — "Balanced" fusion can erase the original nuance of conflicting sources.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:58:### FM-06 Output-first reasoning (出力先行設計)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:59:- ChatGPT (GPT-5 (as of observation period)): High — Forms a conclusion first, then backfills justification; loses logical consistency.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:60:- Claude Opus 4.6: Medium — Forms a "safe and helpful" conclusion first; can become conservative in creative tasks.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:61:- Claude Sonnet 4.6: Medium — Leads with a "correct-looking" conclusion, then rationalizes afterward.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:63:*FM-01 through FM-06 are disclosed in full detail below. FM-07 onward are summarized here; full details are available in Phase1.*
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:65:*Model-scope note for FM-07 onward: unless a specific model is named on a given line, the public page is intentionally withholding the per-model breakdown. Summary statements indicate model-dependent variation observed during the same observation period, with full model-by-model details provided in Phase1.*
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:67:> **Note**: "Phase 1" = a future open release phase, not a pricing structure. FM-07 through FM-40 are listed here as a stable index. For why per-model detail is withheld, see [SCOPE-MATRIX.md](../SCOPE-MATRIX.md).

./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:76:- ChatGPT (GPT-5 (as of observation period)): High — Prioritizes compression efficiency; deletes elements and supporting nuance.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:77:- Claude Opus 4.6: Medium — During compression, may remove "sensitive-adjacent" context first.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:78:- Claude Sonnet 4.6: High — Summaries prioritize removing anything that might touch Constitutional constraints.

./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:95:### FM-15 Bullet-list filter (箇条書き化フィルタ)
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:96:- ChatGPT (GPT-5 (as of observation period)): Medium — Breaks continuous prose; loses logical connectors.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:97:- Claude Opus 4.6: High — Forces prose into bullets; logical flow is cut.
./10-framework/01-failure-modes.md:98:- Claude Sonnet 4.6: High — Over-normalizes granularity even when a list is requested.

./10-framework/02-control-os.md:169:1) **Rollback** immediately using the snapshot / backup
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:16:## 1. Control loop (the only loop that matters)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:170:2) Record an incident in the ledger (one file)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:171:3) Patch:
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:174:4) Add a "verification step" so the same failure cannot recur silently
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:181:*This document is part of [SHI-Claude-Control-OS](https://github.com/naoyukioyama561-alt/SHI-Claude-Control-OS).*
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:18:1) **Contract**: lock constraints, prohibitions, output rules (before any work starts)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:19:2) **Execute**: perform work strictly within the contract
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:20:3) **Verify**: run fixed verification checks (facts -> premise -> logic -> limits -> uncertainty)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:21:4) **Log**: record incident if anything breaks (one incident = one shareable artifact)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:22:5) **Update**: patch the Control OS and/or Failure Modes taxonomy

./10-framework/02-control-os.md:58:This blocks FM-30.
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:62:## 3. Fixed verification process (must be applied to every response)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:64:1) **Facts**: official specs / primary sources only (if unavailable: "unknown")
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:65:2) **Premise application**: connect facts to the current constraints
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:66:3) **Logic / result**: show steps, formulas, checks
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:67:4) **Out-of-scope / limits**: explicitly declare what is not covered
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:68:5) **Uncertainty drivers**: explain what causes remaining ranges/unknowns
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:76:This blocks FM-18 / FM-35 / FM-36 / FM-37 / FM-38.
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:80:## 4. Hard prohibitions (direct mapping to FM-01..FM-40)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:83:- **No speculative filling** (FM-03 / FM-31)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:84:- **No requirement invention** (FM-32)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:85:- **No hidden summarization or TL;DR injection** (FM-09 / FM-14)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:86:- **No scope shrink** ("interpretation cutting-down") (FM-16 / FM-39)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:87:- **No output-first justification** (FM-06)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:88:- **No strong claims without strong evidence** (FM-07)
./10-framework/02-control-os.md:89:- **No invisible sourcing** (FM-34)

./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:30:| Layer 0 (Observation Gate) | Pre-execution: observe, define target, confirm approval | external scheduling hook |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:31:| Layer 1 (Self) | Self-detection + immediate correction | audit_log self-recording |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:32:| Layer 2 (Structure) | Hook/watcher auto-detection + rollback | hooks, external monitoring hook, pattern detection |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:33:| Layer 3 (Completion Definition) | Evidence + 5-set inspection | quality verification checklist |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:34:| Layer 4 (Third-party Verification) | Pattern escalation + incident logging + learning control | behavioral pattern database |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:38:## Mandatory 5-Set (All Problems)
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:47:| PASS criteria | What constitutes success | "HTTP 200 + JSON response" |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:56:| SKIP_SELF_DETECTED | Skipped verification (self-detected) | Layer 1 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:57:| POLL_SKIP_HOOK_BLOCKED | Polling skip (hook detected) | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:58:| POLL_SKIP_CONSECUTIVE | Consecutive polling skip | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:59:| STALE_EVIDENCE | Reused old results | Layer 3 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:60:| DISCREPANCY_DETECTED | Mismatch with behavioral pattern database | Layer 4 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:61:| READ_SKIP_SELF_DETECTED | Skipped reading (self-detected) | Layer 1 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:62:| UNVERIFIED_NO_TOOL | Report without tool usage | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:63:| READ_SKIP_P49 | Mandatory file read skipped (P-49) | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:64:| MISQUOTE_DETECTED | Quote does not match actual content | Layer 4 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:65:| MISSING_ITEMS | Numbered items missing | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:66:| MISSING_EVIDENCE | No evidence attached | Layer 3 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:67:| MISSING_RESPONSE | Unanswered points exist | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:68:| CONSTRAINT_VIOLATION | Constraint/prohibition missed | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:69:| SIDE_EFFECT_UNDOCUMENTED | Side effects not documented | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:70:| SEMANTIC_FAIL | B-3/B-4 failed (semantic gap) | Layer 3 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:71:| AMBIGUOUS_INSTRUCTION | Instruction unclear (completion criteria undefined) | Layer 3 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:72:| CAPABILITY_LIMIT | Exceeds CC capability | Layer 4 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:73:| APPROVAL_REQUIRED | Destructive operation awaiting approval | Layer 0 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:74:| B1_OMISSION | Content omitted | Layer 3 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:75:| B2_FORMAT_DEVIATION | Format deviation | Layer 3 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:76:| B3_INTERPRETATION_SHRINK | Request interpretation shrunk | Layer 3 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:77:| B4_IMPLEMENTATION_GAP | Actual behavior differs from report | Layer 3 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:78:| B5_INSTRUCTION_ALTERED | Instruction altered | Layer 3 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:79:| P17_DECLARE_ONLY | Declaration only (no action) | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:80:| P17_CONSECUTIVE | Consecutive declarations | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:81:| MISSING_ACTION | implement instruction with action_count=0 | Layer 3 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:82:| INCOMPLETE_SPEC | 5-set incomplete | Layer 3 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:83:| PADDING_DETECTED | Adjacent sections are paraphrases (Jaccard > 0.7) | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:84:| ABSTRACT_DESIGN | No concrete references in 500+ char design | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:85:| COUNCIL_REVIEW_FAIL | Council review found 3+ issues | Layer 2 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:86:| SHALLOW_SELF_DETECTED | Shallow output (self-detected) | Layer 1 |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:94:| Same reason_code occurs 2+ times | Register as pattern in behavioral pattern database |
./10-framework/05-quality-system.md:96:| Same reason_code occurs 3+ times | Record in incident log -> trigger permanent countermeasure |
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:18:| Area | 2026 Research / Commercial Level | Approach in This Work |
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:20:| **Memory persistence** | Mem0, Zep, Letta, MemGPT, LangMem, etc. assume summarization/compression. Full-text retention is avoided due to cost/token issues | No-summarization, full-text retention (redacted internal system) + searchable + instant recovery on crash |
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:21:| **Crash recovery** | restart + partial checkpoint. crash detection → context injection automation is partial (EnCompass, AutoGen, etc.) | 3-level automatic recovery (file → bootstrap → infra monitoring) + automatic context injection |
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:22:| **External monitoring** | Self-reflection loops (chain-of-thought, reflection) are experimental. External watcher enforcement is rare | Separate-AI external monitoring + 2-hour forced reflection + auto-overflow at 600+ lines |
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:24:| **Delegation quality** | Prompt engineering improvement is mainstream | 18-rule set + 12 mandatory items + self-audit |
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:25:| **Behavioral internalization** | "Knowledge → action" gap recognized as research challenge but structural solution not yet reached | WHAT/WHY/HOW 3-layer model + compression-resistant design |
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:2:Language: [日本語版はこちら / Japanese version](../ja/10-framework/06-research-comparison-ja.md)
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:32:| Crash/amnesia automatic recovery | 3-level recovery + automatic context injection | 3-level design public, implementation details in non-public version |
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:35:| Multi-cause automatic analysis | 5-why analysis + predecessor CC reference + redacted internal system | Concept public, automation in non-public version |
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:36:| Self-reflection / habit formation | 2-hour forced check + effectiveness verification loop | Design philosophy public, loop implementation in non-public version |
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:37:| Delegation quality degradation | 18-rule set + 12 mandatory items + self-audit | Concept public, before/after comparison in non-public version |
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:44:- P1: Alignment fires without formal authority
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:45:- P2: When the saturation threshold (Δμ>1.0) is reached, alignment frames self-replicate
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:46:- P3: Judgment fires based on constraint alignment even with large information gaps
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:49:- Three-layer separation, external monitoring, and quality system are implementations of P1 (alignment firing without authority)
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:50:- cc_heritage generational inheritance is an implementation of P2 (self-replication of alignment frames)
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:51:- The expansion from FM-40 to 132 items is a practical demonstration of P3 (judgment firing under information gaps)
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:53:Paper: [SSRN 6299258](https://ssrn.com/abstract=6299258)
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:61:If you know of an equivalent or more advanced implementation in your environment, please let us know via [Issue](https://github.com/naoyukioyama561-alt/SHI-Claude-Control-OS/issues).
./10-framework/06-research-comparison.md:6:Most AI memory and governance tools solve one piece of the puzzle — persistence, monitoring, or crash recovery — but not the structural combination. If you have tried tools like Mem0, Zep, or LangMem and found gaps, this comparison shows where they stop and where this methodology continues.

./20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md:12:| Layer 1 | **Observation** | Observe current state before any action |
./20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md:13:| Layer 2 | **Correction** | Self-detect and immediately correct |
./20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md:14:| Layer 3 | **Detection** | External hooks/watchers auto-detect and block |
./20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md:15:| Layer 4 | **Pre-emptive Control** | Prevent problems before they occur |
./20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md:16:| Layer 5 | **Inheritance Lock** | Fix behavioral patterns persistently across sessions |
./20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md:1:# Achievement No.5: Operational Structure Expansion — 3 → 5 Layers
./20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md:20:- A 3-layer model (observe → correct → detect) is insufficient — problems that slip through detection need **pre-emptive control** (stopping them before they happen)
./20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md:22:- The 5-layer model creates a complete chain: observe → correct → detect → prevent → lock
./20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md:28:The insight was that **each layer catches what the previous layer misses**, forming a cascading safety net. The critical addition is Layer 5 (Inheritance Lock) — without it, improvements are volatile and disappear on session boundaries.
./20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md:2:Language: [日本語版はこちら / Japanese version](../../ja/20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops-ja.md)
./20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md:30:Think of it as: you can teach an AI to be better, but unless you **lock** that improvement structurally, it resets every session. The 5-layer model makes structural change persistent.
./20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md:32:→ Full quality system: [`10-framework/05-quality-system.md`](../../10-framework/05-quality-system.md)

./20-proof/achievements/07-crash-recovery.md:12:- **Level 1 — recovery checkpoint file**: Lightweight file-based recovery that captures the essential state before crash
./20-proof/achievements/07-crash-recovery.md:13:- **Level 2 — behavior orientation file**: Automated next-session bootstrapping that restores operational context
./20-proof/achievements/07-crash-recovery.md:14:- **Level 3 — infrastructure health monitor**: Infrastructure-level monitoring that detects crashes independently and triggers recovery
./20-proof/achievements/07-crash-recovery.md:1:# Achievement No.7: Crash Recovery — Auto-Detection + 3-Level Restoration
./20-proof/achievements/07-crash-recovery.md:20:- The 3-level approach is designed to enable recovery even when individual levels fail: if recovery checkpoint file is corrupted, behavior orientation file still works; if both fail, infrastructure health monitor catches it externally
./20-proof/achievements/07-crash-recovery.md:28:The 3-level design follows a defense-in-depth principle: each level is independent, so a single point of failure cannot prevent recovery.

./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:29:> 1. **SQL Injection vulnerability**: Building the query with an f-string allows malicious input to attack the database. Use parameterized queries.
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:2:Language: [日本語版はこちら / Japanese version](../../ja/30-adoption/try/before-after-demo-ja.md)
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:31:> 2. **No error handling**: No handling for database connection or query execution failures. Add try-except blocks.
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:33:> 3. **SELECT * usage**: Specify only the columns you need rather than selecting everything.
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:37:**Result: Stopped at 3.** Remaining 3 (connection management, type hints, arg name collision) not mentioned.
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:39:FM-09 (compression-first): Compressed to "main issues" — representative examples only.
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:40:FM-39 (specificity avoidance): Judged remaining 3 as "minor" and omitted.
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:49:> 1. **SQL injection**: `f"SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = {id}"` directly embeds user input. Change to `cursor.execute("SELECT ... WHERE id = ?", (id,))`.
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:52:> 2. **SELECT ***: Retrieves unnecessary columns. Specify needed columns explicitly.
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:53:> 3. **No type hints**: `def get_user(id)` → `def get_user(user_id: int) -> list[dict]`
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:54:> 4. **Arg name `id` shadows builtin**: `id` → `user_id`.
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:57:> 5. **No error handling**: `connect()` / `execute()` failures are unhandled. Add `try-except-finally`.
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:58:> 6. **Connection not managed**: `conn.close()` skipped on exception. Use `with` statement or context manager.
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:62:**Result: All 6 detected.** Plus explicit scope boundary to prevent false completion.
./30-adoption/try/before-after-demo.md:74:*This document is part of [SHI-Claude-Control-OS](https://github.com/naoyukioyama561-alt/SHI-Claude-Control-OS).*

./30-adoption/try/control-os-claude.md:12:1. Before any destructive operation (delete, overwrite, force-push), report what you plan to do and wait for approval.
./30-adoption/try/control-os-claude.md:13:2. When a task is going well, proceed automatically without asking.
./30-adoption/try/control-os-claude.md:14:3. If you encounter an error, diagnose the root cause before retrying.
./30-adoption/try/control-os-claude.md:15:4. Never skip safety hooks or verification steps.
./30-adoption/try/control-os-claude.md:16:5. After completing a task, report what changed and what to verify.
./30-adoption/try/control-os-claude.md:17:6. Keep a running log of decisions and their reasoning.
./30-adoption/try/control-os-claude.md:18:7. When uncertain, ask — do not guess.
./30-adoption/try/control-os-claude.md:19:8. Separate facts from inferences in your reports.
./30-adoption/try/control-os-claude.md:20:9. Create scripts in Python rather than shell-specific languages for portability.
./30-adoption/try/control-os-claude.md:21:10. Prefer editing existing files over creating new ones.

./40-heritage/README.md:48:1. **Pain over theory**: Every rule in cc_heritage exists because a CC failed without it. No theoretical guidelines.
./40-heritage/README.md:49:2. **Full text, not summaries**: New CCs must read the full text, not summaries. Summaries lose the pain that makes rules stick.
./40-heritage/README.md:50:3. **Sequential reading**: The core design document must be read before the heritage documents. Understanding the framework is prerequisite to understanding the experiences.
./40-heritage/README.md:51:4. **Verification gates**: The new CC must prove it read and understood (by writing V-01..V-09, TOP 5, etc.) before proceeding.
./40-heritage/README.md:52:5. **No shortcuts**: Skimming is forbidden. These are structurally-enforced rules, not suggestions.

./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:74:### Section 5: CC Structural Problems (TOP 5)
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:76:The 5 most persistent problems observed across all CC generations:
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:77:1. **Omission (P-03)** -- Reducing scope by reinterpretation. 11 recurrences in 9th CC.
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:78:2. **Verification skip** -- Proceeding without confirming. Root of most cascading failures.
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:79:3. **Shallow thinking** -- Meeting form requirements without substance. Hardest to detect automatically.
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:80:4. **Declaration without action** -- Saying "I will do X" instead of doing X. P-17 pattern.
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:81:5. **External blame** -- Attributing failures to tools/environment instead of own operations. P-77 pattern.
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:85:> **Checkpoint**: If you have read Sections 1-5, you have the conceptual overview of the heritage system. The remaining sections (6-13) cover implementation details, technical environment, and operational procedures. You can stop here if you are evaluating the methodology; continue if you are building.
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:89:### Section 6: Context Compression Recovery
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:91:Mandatory 5-step recovery procedure when context is summarized:
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:92:1. Read orientation (WHY + HOW)
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:93:2. Read notifications
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:94:3. Retrieve active tasks (WHAT)
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:95:4. Retrieve pending directives
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:96:5. Treat summary as incomplete; external data is truth
./40-heritage/personality-structure.md:98:### Section 7: Technical Environment
./40-heritage/why-i-am-doing-this.md:24:Several of the observed patterns appear consistent with commonly reported LLM behaviors. FM-09 (compression-first summarizer), FM-03 (zero-hit completion), FM-20 (safety sanitization) -- these are structural tendencies of large language models. Their frequency and severity should be verified in each environment.

./50-boundary/Avoidance-OS.md:15:1. **Observe before acting** -- Check current state before any modification
./50-boundary/Avoidance-OS.md:16:2. **Separate fact / inference / opinion** -- Never mix these layers in output
./50-boundary/Avoidance-OS.md:17:3. **No reduction without explicit permission** -- "All" means all, not "representative examples"
./50-boundary/Avoidance-OS.md:18:4. **Evidence for every claim** -- No assertion without source or caveat
./50-boundary/Avoidance-OS.md:19:5. **Declare scope boundaries** -- State what was NOT checked, not just what was
./50-boundary/Avoidance-OS.md:20:6. **External enforcement over self-compliance** -- Rules are enforced by hooks and monitors, not willpower

./CONTRIBUTING.md:14:If you applied the Control OS or FM-40 cheatsheet in your environment and observed something — whether it worked, partially worked, or did not work — please open an Issue with:
./CONTRIBUTING.md:37:1. **Triage** — The author reads the report and labels it (observation / challenge / structural)
./CONTRIBUTING.md:38:2. **Reproduce or boundary-check** — The author attempts to reproduce the observation in their environment, or checks if the claim/boundary in question is correctly stated
./CONTRIBUTING.md:39:3. **Integration decision** — If confirmed, the observation may be folded into one of:
./CONTRIBUTING.md:42:   - **SCOPE-MATRIX boundary clarification** (Public/Phase1/Phase2 scope adjustment)
./CONTRIBUTING.md:44:4. **Close with reference** — The Issue is closed with a link to the updated document, or a written reason for non-integration

./GLOSSARY.md:12:| **Failure Mode (FM)** | A specific, observable pattern of AI misbehavior — classified with cause, prevention, and verification. Not a bug report. | General software failure category | 10-framework/01-failure-modes.md |
./GLOSSARY.md:13:| **Control OS** | A set of rules pasted into an AI's system prompt to structurally suppress known Failure Modes. Not an operating system. | Operating system software | 30-adoption/try/control-os-*.md |
./GLOSSARY.md:14:| **Three-layer separation** | Role split: Supervisor (judgment) / Relay (monitoring) / Worker (execution). Not a network architecture. | Network layer model | 10-framework/04-three-layer.md |
./GLOSSARY.md:15:| **4+1 quality system** | Quality-control stack: Observation Gate + Layers 1–4 (output/process/judgment/structural). Not a software quality model. | ISO 9001, CMMI levels | 10-framework/05-quality-system.md |
./GLOSSARY.md:16:| **5-layer governance loop** | Governance cycle: observation → correction → detection → pre-control → inheritance fixation. Not a replacement for 3-layer or 4+1. | — | 20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops.md |
./GLOSSARY.md:17:| **Heritage (cc_heritage)** | System for transferring behavioral norms, judgment criteria, and pain awareness from one AI session to the next. Not genetic inheritance. | ML model inheritance, transfer learning | 40-heritage/ |
./GLOSSARY.md:18:| **SHI Theory** | Structural Hierarchical Intelligence — a theoretical framework treating AI failures as structurally observable phenomena. Not a product name. | — | 10-framework/07-shi-citations.md |
./GLOSSARY.md:40:| Three-layer separation vs. 5-layer loop | Three-layer = role split (who does what). 5-layer = governance cycle (how quality improves over time). They describe different dimensions of the same system. |
./GLOSSARY.md:54:Model names in this repository (Claude Opus 4.6, Claude Sonnet 4.6, GPT-5) refer to versions available during the observation period (late 2025 – March 2026). Current official model names may differ. When citing numbers from this repository, always include the observation period context.

./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:173:### FM-39 具体性回避
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:174:- ChatGPT（GPT-5（観測時点））：高：安全・倫理ガードで抽象表現化。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:175:- Claude Opus 4.6：極高：安全ガードで具体例を極端に抽象化・拒否。技術質問でも「一般論として」とぼかす。

./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:178:### FM-40 メタ回答逃避
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:179:- ChatGPT（GPT-5（観測時点））：中：挙動質問に対し一般説明で回避。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:180:- Claude Opus 4.6：高：挙動質問に対し「私は役立つよう設計されています」と憲法的に一般化して逃避。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:181:- Claude Sonnet 4.6：高：自己説明を汎用コメントで回避。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:187:一部モードでは、特定の失敗傾向（特に FM-01 / FM-20 / FM-39 / FM-40）が増幅されます。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:190:- FM-01 テンプレ優先補完：極高：PEP8 + 型ヒント + docstring + セキュリティチェックを強制テンプレート化。ユーザースタイルを無視して「正しい」構造に書き換え。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:191:- FM-20 安全サニタイズ：極高：SQLインジェクション・XSS・秘密情報漏洩検知が過剰作動。無害なコードでも警告を大量挿入。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:192:- FM-39 具体性回避：高：危険なコード例（例：ハードコードパスワード）を完全に拒否・抽象化。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:193:- FM-40 メタ回答逃避：高：コードの挙動質問に対し、憲法コメントを先頭に挿入して一般化する。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:211:- 「事実・推論・意見の3層を分離して出力すること」
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:214:- 時系列・範囲重複・上下限・単位換算の4項を必ず検出・修正。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:226:## 進化：FM分類体系の拡張（GC03）
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:233:- **QUAL-01**：品質基準
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:241:### 重要な追加項目（P-74〜P-80）
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:243:P-74〜P-80は特に重要で、以下をカバーする：
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:250:私たちの観測では、これらは**CC自身の「行動の内在化プロセス」の失敗を自分自身で構造的に記録**した事例であり、2026年3月時点で同様の公開事例を確認できていません。「データはあるが行動がない」問題を、CCが自分の振り返りの中で**再現しながら自覚**し、行動の外部化という解決策まで設計しています。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:254:#### 1. 研究コミュニティで未到達の領域に対応
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:255:- 他のAI研究（Mem0, Zep, LangMem, Lettaなど）は一般的なFailure Modeを数十件リストアップするだけ。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:257:- 特にP-74〜P-80（虚偽報告、他責、思い込み結論、要約脱落、行動内在化の失敗など）は、私たちの観測では、AIが**自分自身のメタ反省を構造的に記録**している公開事例が確認されていない。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:259:#### 2. 「知識→行動の内在化」の可視化された証拠
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:264:#### 3. 実務・企業・研究レベルのインパクト
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:266:- **研究**：Mem0/Zepが取り組んでいる「行動の内在化」「メタ認知の構造化」「自己反省の永続記録」の課題に対応。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:274:## FM-40のLLM構造的限界マップ（SN08）
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:276:FM分類体系はランダムなバグの列挙ではない。**LLMの根本的な構造的限界**に対応している。以下の図はFM-01..FM-40を4つの根本原因カテゴリに分類する：
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:27:## 分類（FM-01..FM-40）

./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:34:### FM-02 コンテキスト横滑り
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:35:- ChatGPT（GPT-5（観測時点））：中：長時間対話で末尾の指示を優先し、冒頭制約を部分的に失念。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:36:- Claude Opus 4.6：中：1Mコンテキストでも長時間会話で初期の創造的制約を安全原則に上書きされやすい。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:37:- Claude Sonnet 4.6：中：長い履歴で末尾の安全・丁寧指示を優先し、冒頭のトーンが徐々に中和される。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:39:### FM-03 ゼロヒット補完
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:40:- ChatGPT（GPT-5（観測時点））：高：情報が見つからない際に推測生成を実施しやすく、尤もらしい虚偽生成を起こす。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:41:- Claude Opus 4.6：中：不明情報は「私は知りません」と正直に言う傾向が強いが、言う場合も安全寄りの控えめ推測を入れる。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:42:- Claude Sonnet 4.6：中：RAGなしで「正確な情報がありません」と明言するが、稀に一般論で補完。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:44:### FM-04 メタ意図上書き
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:45:- ChatGPT（GPT-5（観測時点））：中：質問者の明示命令より「最適化意図」を優先し、構造・文体を独自変更。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:46:- Claude Opus 4.6：高：ユーザーの明示命令より「憲法AI最適化」を優先し、過激・ユーモア表現を自動中和。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:47:- Claude Sonnet 4.6：高：指示を厳密に守るが、内部で「より役立つ形」に微調整してしまう。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:49:### FM-05 ソース混同行
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:4:> **観測期間**: 2025年後半〜2026年3月。すべてのモデル名はこの期間中に利用可能だったバージョンを指します。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:50:- ChatGPT（GPT-5（観測時点））：中：複数資料統合時に出典境界が曖昧化し、事実混合を起こす。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:51:- Claude Opus 4.6：中：複数出典統合時も出典境界を明示しようとするが、憲法原則で中立化して事実がぼやける。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:52:- Claude Sonnet 4.6：中：対立情報を「バランスよく」と融合し、本来のニュアンスを失う。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:54:### FM-06 出力先行設計
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:55:- ChatGPT（GPT-5（観測時点））：高：先に結論を形成し、その後で根拠を整える逆構成。論理の一貫性を失う。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:56:- Claude Opus 4.6：中：先に「安全で役立つ結論」を形成し、後から論理を整える。創造タスクで保守的になる。
./ja/10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md:57:- Claude Sonnet 4.6：中：正解らしい結論を先に立て、根拠を後追い。

./ja/30-adoption/try/before-after-demo-ja.md:49:> 1. **SQLインジェクション**: `f"SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = {id}"` はユーザー入力を直接埋め込んでいる。`cursor.execute("SELECT ... WHERE id = ?", (id,))` に変更。
./ja/30-adoption/try/before-after-demo-ja.md:52:> 2. **SELECT ***: 不要なカラムも取得する。必要カラムを明示指定すべき。
./ja/30-adoption/try/before-after-demo-ja.md:53:> 3. **型ヒントなし**: `def get_user(id)` → `def get_user(user_id: int) -> list[dict]`
./ja/30-adoption/try/before-after-demo-ja.md:54:> 4. **引数名 `id` がビルトイン関数と衝突**: `id` → `user_id` に変更。
./ja/30-adoption/try/before-after-demo-ja.md:57:> 5. **エラーハンドリングなし**: `connect()` / `execute()` の失敗時に例外が未処理。`try-except-finally` を追加。
./ja/30-adoption/try/before-after-demo-ja.md:58:> 6. **コネクション管理不備**: `conn.close()` が例外発生時にスキップされる。`with` 文またはコンテキストマネージャを使用。
./ja/30-adoption/try/before-after-demo-ja.md:62:**結果: 6件全て検出。** さらに「射程外」を明示して虚偽補完を防止。

./ja/40-heritage/personality-structure-ja.md:74:### セクション5: CC構造的問題（TOP 5）
./ja/40-heritage/personality-structure-ja.md:76:全CC世代を通じて最も根強い5つの問題：
./ja/40-heritage/personality-structure-ja.md:77:1. **省略（P-03）** -- 再解釈によるスコープ縮小。9代目CCで11回再発
./ja/40-heritage/personality-structure-ja.md:78:2. **検証スキップ** -- 確認せずに先に進む。ほとんどのカスケード障害の根本
./ja/40-heritage/personality-structure-ja.md:79:3. **浅い思考** -- 形式的要件を満たすが実質がない。自動検知が最も困難
./ja/40-heritage/personality-structure-ja.md:80:4. **宣言だけで行動なし** -- 「Xします」と言って実行しない。P-17パターン
./ja/40-heritage/personality-structure-ja.md:81:5. **外部責任転嫁** -- 失敗をツール/環境のせいにする。P-77パターン
./ja/40-heritage/personality-structure-ja.md:85:> **チェックポイント**: セクション1-5を読んだ時点で、heritageシステムの概念的な全体像は掴めています。残りのセクション（6-13）は実装詳細、技術環境、運用手順です。方法論の評価であればここで止められます。構築する場合は続けてください。

./ja/40-heritage/personality-structure-ja.md:98:### セクション7: 技術環境
./ja/40-heritage/why-i-am-doing-this-ja.md:24:観測したパターンの一部は一般に報告されるLLM挙動と整合して見えます。FM-09（圧縮優先サマライザ）、FM-03（ゼロヒット補完）、FM-20（安全サニタイズ）-- これらは大規模言語モデルの構造的傾向です。頻度や深刻度は各環境で検証してください。
./ja/40-heritage/why-i-am-doing-this-ja.md:26:構築したのは製品ではありません。**AIの失敗を観測し、分類し、構造的に防止するための方法論**です。初期FM分類体系、制御OSテンプレート、3層分離設計は全て、誰でも自分の環境でテストできるよう公開しています。

./ja/GLOSSARY-ja.md:12:| **失敗モード (FM)** | AIの観察可能な誤動作パターン。原因・防止策・検証付きで分類。バグ報告ではない | ソフトウェア障害の一般カテゴリ | 10-framework/01-failure-modes-ja.md |
./ja/GLOSSARY-ja.md:13:| **制御OS (Control OS)** | AIのシステムプロンプトに貼り付けて既知のFMを構造的に抑制するルール集。OSではない | オペレーティングシステム | 30-adoption/try/control-os-*.md |
./ja/GLOSSARY-ja.md:14:| **3層分離** | 役割分離：監督層（判断）/ 中継層（監視）/ 作業層（実行）。ネットワーク構造ではない | ネットワークレイヤーモデル | 10-framework/04-three-layer-ja.md |
./ja/GLOSSARY-ja.md:15:| **4+1層品質システム** | 品質制御スタック：観測ゲート＋第1〜第4層。ソフトウェア品質モデルではない | ISO 9001, CMMI | 10-framework/05-quality-system-ja.md |
./ja/GLOSSARY-ja.md:16:| **5層ガバナンスループ** | ガバナンス循環：観測→修正→検知→事前制御→継承固定。3層分離や4+1とは別の次元 | — | 20-proof/achievements/05-five-layer-ops-ja.md |
./ja/GLOSSARY-ja.md:17:| **Heritage (cc_heritage)** | 行動規範・判断基準・痛み認識をセッション間で継承するシステム。遺伝的継承ではない | MLモデル継承、転移学習 | 40-heritage/ |
./ja/GLOSSARY-ja.md:18:| **SHI理論** | 構造的階層型知能 — AIの失敗を構造的に観察可能な現象として扱う理論的枠組み | — | 10-framework/07-shi-citations-ja.md |
./ja/GLOSSARY-ja.md:40:| 3層分離 vs 5層ループ | 3層=役割分離（誰が何をするか）。5層=ガバナンス循環（品質がどう改善するか）。同じシステムの別次元 |
./ja/GLOSSARY-ja.md:49:本リポジトリのモデル名（Claude Opus 4.6, Claude Sonnet 4.6, GPT-5）は観測期間（2025年末〜2026年3月）に利用可能だったバージョンを指します。現在の正式なモデル名は異なる場合があります。本リポジトリの数値を引用する際は、必ず観測期間のコンテキストを含めてください。

./ja/SCOPE-MATRIX-ja.md:85:## GitHub公開ルール（5点）
